 In Kashmir's Budgam district two days ago, a policeman absconding with a service rifle reported that he had become a member of the terrorist organization Hizbul Mujahideen
 jammu-kashmir police kaa sipaahi said navid mushtak chandpura ilaake se chaar insaas rifl ke saath faraar ho gaya tha, jahaan use bhartiya khaadya nigam (epasiai) ke godaam kii raksha main tainaat kiya gaya tha
 "we welcome Saeed Naveed (mushtaq) Shah," local media quoted Burhan Uddin as spokesman for Hizbul Mujahideen
 police ke ek adhikari ne bataaya ki khufia soochna ke mutabik mushtakatankwaadi samoohamen shaamil ho gaya tha
 Mushtaq joined the police force in 2012, who absconded last Saturday with his and three other colleagues' INSAS rifles
 pulicekarmiyon ke sarvice rifl ke saath faraar hone or vibhinn aatankwaadi sanghathanon main shaamil hone ke maamle badhate ja rahe hai
 About a year ago, policeman Shakur Ahmed absconded with four rifles and reportedly joined the militant organization
 use kareeb dedh maheene baad kulgaam se giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 Earlier, Pulwama district soldier Naseer Ahmed Pandit escaped from the residence of PDP minister Altaf Bukhari on 27 March 2015 with two AK rifles

 What happens NEFT service NEFT means that the settlement of fund transfer is done at a certain time under National Electronic Fund Transfer

 ravivaar va chuttee vaale din yah sarvice nahin milti he

 ise online or bank branch donon madhyamon se istemaal kiya ja saktaa he

 Where the White House stands today, it was once a jungle-mountain

 3
 Although there have been some changes to the White House map over 200 years of history, the map of the White House is largely the same today as it once was
 is nakshe ke mutabik white house ke purab kii taraf manoranjan ke liye ek imaarat he
 The three parlors on the south side are Green, Blue and Red Parlors
 inhen parloron main white house kii pahchaan ovel digaayan vaala daftar he
 On the west side is the State Dining Hall
 uttar kii taraf wo imaaraten hai jahaan raashtrapati kaa parivaar rahata he
 4
 1812 ke yuddh main british fouj ne washington par kabja kar liya tha, iske baad usne white house ko bhi aag ke hawaale kar diya tha
 Those traces of fire are still found at the White House under several layers of paint when it is painted
 white house ke vidhwans ke fouran baad hi raashtrapati james maron ne white house ke punirmaan kaa aadesh diya tha
 The White House has since been the permanent residence of US presidents
 5
 White house is built in white sandstone in Georgian style
 jon adams ke kaarykaal se hi yah american raashtrapati kaa sarkari awaas he

 Baru has mentioned his memoirs in the Prime Minister's Office in this book
 yah pustak ek tarah se bijepi ke un aaropon kii pushti karti he ki manmohan singh behad kamazor pradhanmantri the or satta kaa sanchaalan congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi ke haathon main tha
 Baru writes in this book that Manmohan Singh himself believed that there could not be two centers of power, hence he gave the right to take all decisions to Sonia Gandhi
 kitaab main yah daawa bhi kiya gaya he ki faisle lene se pehle kai mahatvapurn filein sonia gandhi ko dikhaai jaati thim
 However, the Prime Minister's Office and the Congress have rejected Baru's claims
 congress kaa kahana he ki baru ne apni kitaab kii bikri badhaane ke liye ain chunaavon ke bich ye sansanikhej daawey kiye hai
 Even before this, journalists who were media advisors to the Prime Minister have been putting forth their experiences through books
 purv pradhanmantri indira gandhi or rajeev gandhi ke media salaahkaar rahe echvaay sharada prasad or laal bahadur shastri ke media salaahkaar rahe kuldeep naiyyar kii pustaken bhi saamne ai hai, lekin shaayad itnaa vivaad pehle kabhi nahin hua
 The revelations made in Baru's book have been taken up by nda's prime ministerial candidate Narendra Modi
 unhone iske hawaale se sonia gandhi kii chuppi par sawaal uthaaya he or baru ke daawey par safai maangi he ki vah sarkari filein dekhati rahi hai
 There is a lot of speculation about Baru's book in political corridors
 kuch log yah bhi kah rahe hai ki is kitaab ke zarie baru ne manmohan singh ko upie ke duusare kaarykaal kii naakaamiyon se dur rakhane kii koshish kii he
 So far, it has come that the Congress party blamed Manmohan Singh for every dispute, then the success of each succession tied the heads of Sonia Gandhi and Rahul Gandhi
 baru kii yah kitaab yah sabit karne kii koshish karti he ki tamaam vivaadon main manmohan singh kii sidhe taur par koi bhoomika nahin rahi he
 The differences between Congress Party and Manmohan Singh over the inclusion of controversial leaders in the Cabinet and the nuclear deal with the US have also been highlighted prominently in this book
 dilachasp baat yah he ki congress ke mahasachiv digvijay singh satta ke do kendron ke prayog ke asafal hone kii baat kahkar vivaad khadaa kar chuke hai, lekin baru kii yah kitaab is baat ko sire se khaarij karti he
 Baru clearly states that there is only one center of power and that is Sonia Gandhi
 is tarah se pradhanmantri ke purv media salaahkaar or unke behad kareebi rahe sanjay baru ne loksabhaa chunaavon ke sambhavit parinaamon ke liye rahul gandhi-sonia gandhi ke bajaae manmohan singh ko zimmedaar tehraane kii congress kii koshishon par abhi se pani pher diya he
 Baru's book comes at a time when the investigation of coal scam is reaching the Prime Minister's Office
 sibiai ne pradhanmantri karyaalay main purv pramukh sachiv rahe or philhal bataur salaahkaar kaam kar rahe tikee nair se poochtacha kii he
 Those close to Manmohan Singh fear that if the UPA does not return to power, it should not be that Manmohan Singh is also taken into the custody of this investigation
 shaayad yahi vajah he ki baru kii yah kitaab kai mahatvapurn or vivaadaaspad faislon se manmohan singh kii duuri ko rekhaankit karti he
 Among these, there is mention of Manmohan Singh's opposition to taking TR Balu and a Raja into the cabinet when the government was formed in 2009

 Ashok Singhal, a metallurgist engineer who took up the issue of Hindutva and played an important role in the Ram Mandir movement, was in the last years of the 1980s and later nationally
 unhone bijepi ke netritv vaale is raajnneetik andolan main vishwa hindu parishad (viechpi) ke adhyaksh ke rup main ahm bhoomika nibhaai

 unhone aakraamak style apanaate hue ram janmabhumi or ram sethu andolanon ke liye logon ko ekajute karne main pramukh bhoomika nibhaai

 Born on 2 October 1926 in Agra, Singhal earned a bachelor's degree in metallurgical engineering from the 'institute of Technology' of Banaras Hindu University in 1950
 vah saal 1942 main rashtriya swayamsevak sangh se jud gaye the, lekin snaatak kii padhai puri karne ke baad vah purnakalik prachaarak bane
 He worked in several places in Uttar Pradesh and became a pracharak of Delhi and Haryana
 saal 1980 main unhen viechpi main jimmedaari dete hue iskaa sanyukt mahasachiv banaaya gaya
 He became its General Secretary in the year 1984 and was later appointed as its Executive Chairman
 is pad par vah disambar 2011 tak rahe
 He was inspired by the ideology of RSS throughout his life and was a prominent member of the Sangh Parivar
 biechpi netaa singhl ko apana 'maardarshak' maanate the, kyonki unhone apane jeevankaal main kai andolanon kaa netritv kiya
 Singhal contributed significantly in the movement against the Emergency in Uttar Pradesh and in starting the 'gau Raksha Andolan' to protect the cows
 singhl viechpi main sakriy rahe or ant tak iske sangrakshak rahe
 a few days before hospitalization, Singhal made a 30-day tour of various countries to see the functioning of the VHP

 5: padhai ke dauraan hi kshitij reppertery or shri ram centre (dilli) se rajkumaar raav theatre bhi kiya karte the
 6: Rajkumar Rao also graduated from Delhi's Film and Television Institute of India after Delhi and moved to Mumbai
 film institute se aane ke baad, mumbai main rajkumaar ko pehla brake dibaakar banerjee kii film 'lav sex or dhokhaa' main mila
 7: After that Rajkumar also did Ekta Kapoor's 'ragini MMS' and he got much appreciation
 uske baad film 'shaitan' main bhi rajkumaar raav kaa ahm role tha
 8: After these films, Rajkumar played small roles in the films 'gangs of Wasseypur 2', 'chitgong' and 'talaash'
 uske baad rajkumaar raav ne 'kaay po che', 'city lits', 'queen' or 'doli kii doli' jaisi filmon main bhi apana haath aajamaaya
 9: Rajkummar Rao's film 'shahid' was also awarded the National Award
 10; rajkumaar kii nijee jindagi main abhinetri 'patralekha' kaa ahm sthaan he or donon ek duusare ke saath zyada se zyada vakt vyateet karnaa pasand karte hai
 UP Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath on Friday in Panchayat Aaj Tak presented the blueprint of his formula to make Uttar Pradesh a 'perfect state'
 unhone kanoon vyavastha se lekar saamaajik sadbhaav tak sab par apni baat rakhi
 Read the complete speech of Yogi Adityanath
 
 
 100 din baad duungaa report cardyogi adityanathane apane sambodhan main kaha ki bijepi ko desh ke pradhanmantri modi ke netritv main upi kii janata ne prachand janadesh diya he
 Will meet the expectations and aspirations of 22 crore people of UP
 mujhe lagata he ki dedh maheene main parivartan dikhaai diya hoga
 You must have seen that if CM changes, then people start shoving the administration
 hamane ek maheene baad parivartan kii shuruyaat kii
 We tried to change there
 jahaan log badalane ko taiyaar nahin the
 The Prime Minister gave us the mantra that everyone should be with everyone
 uttar pradesh kaa jangalraj samaapt hoga or aapako yah dikhaai de rahaa hoga
 i will come to the media 100 days later with the government report
 transfar par kya bole CM yogiuttar pradesh ko bimaaru rajya kii shrenee se baharlana hamaari praathamikta he
 Law and order was the first priority in UP and we are working on it
 nai transfar policy lekar aae hai
 The transfer and posting industry was done and no one would be able to do so here
 kisi ko kyon hataaya ja rahaa he
 On this, along with informing the minister, the officer will have to tell me and its accountability will also be decided
 is team work ke saath jo chalegaa, wo rah paaegaa
 And who does not like it
 agar wo hamase kahegaa to ham use ghar tak pahunchane kii vyavastha karenge
 Will end for VIP Sanskritikasan also
 naujavaanon ke liye bhi or yahaan kii buniyadi vyavasthaaon ke liye bhi viipi samskruti khatm hogi
 Criminal people will not get protection at the level of governance
 apradhi ko kanoon haath main lene kii ijaajat nahinhai
 Those taking over the law will be dealt with vigorously
 kisaanon par kya boleuttar pradesh kaa kisaan badahaal hua he
 Nature is full of grace on UP, but the farmer is in a bad state and it has become a misfortune for him to choose a path like suicide
 hamane kisaanon ke hit ko dhyaan main rakhte hue karj se raahat dene ke liye fasali rin ko maaf kiya he
 Yield benefits for sustainable profit
 iskaa upaay kiya gaya he
 An initiative has been taken to provide support price to the farmer so that he tries to double his income by becoming self-sufficient
 hamane 5 hajaar genhu kray khole hai
 Till last year, grain was purchased from agents and agents
 aapane dekha hoga pichley varsh tak kisaanon ko samarthan mulya bhi nahin mil paata tha
 Farmer's money should not stop anywhere
 aisi vyavastha ham bana rahe hai
 We will buy grain directly from the farmer
 market main gehun kaa daam samarthan mulya se zyada he
 If no one is going to buy, the government will buy
 ganna kisaanon ke liye kya bolegnna kisaanon ke liye ganna mulya kaa bhugtan ho chukaa he
 Over 6000 crore has been paid
